    <script>
        // Theme toggle
        const html = document.getElementById('html-root');
        const themeToggle = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
        
        const logoDark = 'img/LOGO FAST PROXY.png';
        const logoLight = 'https://i.ibb.co/ymxkPNS0/LOGO-FAST-PROXY-black.png';
        
        function updateLogos() {
            const logos = document.querySelectorAll('.logo-img');
            const isDark = html.classList.contains('dark');
            logos.forEach(logo => {
                logo.src = isDark ? logoDark : logoLight;
            });
        }
        
        themeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            html.classList.toggle('dark');
            html.classList.toggle('light');
            updateLogos();
            localStorage.setItem('theme', html.classList.contains('dark') ? 'dark' : 'light');
        });

        // Load saved theme
        if (localStorage.getItem('theme')) {
            html.classList.remove('dark', 'light');
            html.classList.add(localStorage.getItem('theme'));
            updateLogos();
        }

        // Mobile menu
        const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-btn');
        const mobileMenuClose = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-close');
        const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
        const mobileOverlay = document.getElementById('mobile-overlay');

        function openMobileMenu() {
            mobileMenu.classList.add('active');
            mobileOverlay.classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }

        function closeMobileMenu() {
            mobileMenu.classList.remove('active');
            mobileOverlay.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', openMobileMenu);
        mobileMenuClose.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
        mobileOverlay.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);

        // Close mobile menu on link click
        document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-menu a').forEach(link => {
            link.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
        });

        // Plan type toggle
        const planToggleBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.plan-toggle-btn');
        planToggleBtns.forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                planToggleBtns.forEach(b => {
                    b.classList.remove('active');
                    if (html.classList.contains('dark')) {
                        b.style.background = 'transparent';
                        b.style.color = '#9ca3af';
                    } else {
                        b.style.background = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
                        b.style.color = '#52525b';
                    }
                });
                btn.classList.add('active');
                btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #22c55e, #16a34a)';
                btn.style.color = 'white';
                
                const type = btn.dataset.type;
                if (type === 'onepurchase') {
                    html.classList.add('show-onepurchase');
                } else {
                    html.classList.remove('show-onepurchase');
                }
            });
        });

        // Reveal on scroll
        const reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    entry.target.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.1 });

        reveals.forEach(el => observer.observe(el));

        // Navbar scroll effect
        const navbar = document.getElementById('navbar');
        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });

        // Checkout Modal
        let currentPeriod = 'monthly';
        let currentType = 'ipv6';
        let basePrice = 29.90;

        // Home Page Type Selector
        const HOME_PRICING = {
            ipv6:   { name: 'IPv6',        icon: 'ðŸŒ', minQty: 1, sellPrice: 29.90, autoDelivery: false },
            ipv4:   { name: 'IPv4',        icon: 'ðŸ–¥ï¸', minQty: 1, sellPrice: 39.90, autoDelivery: true  },
            isp:    { name: 'ISP',         icon: 'ðŸ¢', minQty: 1, sellPrice: 49.90, autoDelivery: true  },
            mobile: { name: 'Mobile 4G/5G',icon: 'ðŸ“±', minQty: 1, sellPrice: 79.90, autoDelivery: true  }
        };

        const HOME_PERIODS = [
            { id: '1m',  name: '1 MÃªs',    months: 1,  discount: 0    },
            { id: '6m',  name: '6 Meses',  months: 6,  discount: 0.25 },
            { id: '12m', name: '12 Meses', months: 12, discount: 0.35 }
        ];

        let panelSelectedPeriod = '1m';

        function showMobileComingSoon() {
            showToast('Mobile 4G/5G em breve! Fique ligado nas novidades.', 'info');
        }

        function selectHomeType(type) {
            // Block mobile plan â€” coming soon
            if (type === 'mobile') { showMobileComingSoon(); return; }

            currentType = type;

            // On mobile (< 768px): open bottom-sheet instead of scrolling to panel
            if (window.innerWidth < 768) {
                openMobilePricingSheet(type);
                return;
            }

            // Desktop: update type card highlights + purchase panel
            document.querySelectorAll('.plan-type-card').forEach(card => {
                card.classList.remove('selected-type');
                card.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                card.style.background  = 'var(--bg-card)';
            });
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`type-card-${type}`);
            if (activeCard) activeCard.classList.add('selected-type');

            updatePurchasePanel();

            // Smooth-scroll to the purchase panel
            const panel = document.getElementById('home-purchase-panel');
            if (panel) panel.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
        }

        function updatePurchasePanel() {
            const info = HOME_PRICING[currentType];

            document.getElementById('panel-type-icon').textContent = info.icon;
            document.getElementById('panel-type-name').textContent = info.name;
            document.getElementById('panel-type-tag').textContent  = `R$${info.sellPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')} por proxy/mÃªs`;

            const badge = document.getElementById('panel-delivery-badge');
            if (!info.autoDelivery) {
                badge.textContent  = 'ðŸ“¦ Estoque';
                badge.className    = 'text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 font-semibold';
            } else {
                badge.textContent  = 'âš¡ API Auto';
                badge.className    = 'text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 font-semibold';
            }

            // Show quantity selector for ALL types
            const qtySection = document.getElementById('panel-qty-section');
            qtySection.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('panel-qty').min   = info.minQty;
            document.getElementById('panel-qty').value = info.minQty;

            updatePanelTotal();
        }

        function selectPanelPeriod(periodId) {
            panelSelectedPeriod = periodId;

            HOME_PERIODS.forEach(p => {
                const btn = document.getElementById(`panel-period-${p.id}`);
                if (!btn) return;
                if (p.id === periodId) {
                    btn.style.borderColor = '#22c55e';
                    btn.style.background  = 'rgba(34,197,94,0.1)';
                } else {
                    btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                    btn.style.background  = '';
                }
            });

            updatePanelTotal();
        }

        function changePanelQty(delta) {
            const input  = document.getElementById('panel-qty');
            const minVal = parseInt(input.min) || 1;
            input.value  = Math.max(minVal, parseInt(input.value || 1) + delta);
            updatePanelTotal();
        }

        function updatePanelTotal() {
            const info    = HOME_PRICING[currentType];
            const period  = HOME_PERIODS.find(p => p.id === panelSelectedPeriod) || HOME_PERIODS[0];
            const qty     = parseInt(document.getElementById('panel-qty').value) || 1;

            const pricePerMonth = info.sellPrice * (1 - period.discount);
            const total         = pricePerMonth * period.months * qty;

            document.getElementById('panel-total').textContent    = `R$ ${total.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            document.getElementById('panel-price-pm').textContent = `R$ ${info.sellPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}${period.discount > 0 ? ` (âˆ’${Math.round(period.discount * 100)}%)` : ''}`;
        }

        let homePendingPurchase = null;

        function startHomePurchase() {
            const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('panel-qty').value) || 1;
            homePendingPurchase = {
                type:     currentType,
                period:   panelSelectedPeriod,
                quantity: qty,
                months:   (HOME_PERIODS.find(p => p.id === panelSelectedPeriod) || HOME_PERIODS[0]).months
            };
            openHomeTermsModal();
        }

        function openHomeTermsModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('home-terms-modal');
            if (!modal) return;
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            document.getElementById('home-terms-checkbox').checked = false;
            document.getElementById('home-continue-btn').disabled = true;
        }

        function toggleHomeTermsCheckbox() {
            const checked = document.getElementById('home-terms-checkbox').checked;
            document.getElementById('home-continue-btn').disabled = !checked;
        }

        function closeHomeTermsModal() {
            document.getElementById('home-terms-modal').classList.add('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function acceptHomeTermsAndContinue() {
            if (!document.getElementById('home-terms-checkbox').checked) {
                showToast('VocÃª precisa aceitar os termos para continuar', 'error');
                return;
            }
            closeHomeTermsModal();
            // Route through the unauthenticated Stripe checkout modal (email + whatsapp â†’ /api/stripe/create-checkout)
            setTimeout(() => openCheckoutModalWithData(
                homePendingPurchase.type,
                homePendingPurchase.period,
                homePendingPurchase.quantity
            ), 300);
        }

        function openHomeBuyerModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('home-buyer-modal');
            if (!modal) return;
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-name').value = '';
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-document').value = '';
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-whatsapp').value = '';
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-address').value = '';
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-name').focus();
        }

        function closeHomeBuyerModal() {
            document.getElementById('home-buyer-modal').classList.add('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function backToHomeTerms() {
            closeHomeBuyerModal();
            setTimeout(() => openHomeTermsModal(), 300);
        }

        document.getElementById('home-buyer-form')?.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            const token = localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_token');
            if (!token) {
                showToast('FaÃ§a login para comprar', 'error');
                setTimeout(() => window.location.href = '/portal.html', 1500);
                return;
            }

            const name = document.getElementById('home-buyer-name').value.trim();
            const document_ = document.getElementById('home-buyer-document').value.trim();
            const whatsapp = document.getElementById('home-buyer-whatsapp').value.trim();
            const address = document.getElementById('home-buyer-address').value.trim();
            
            if (!name || !document_ || !whatsapp) {
                showToast('Preencha todos os campos obrigatÃ³rios', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            showToast('Criando checkout...', 'info');
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/checkout/create-checkout-session', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ 
                        type: homePendingPurchase.type, 
                        period: homePendingPurchase.period, 
                        quantity: homePendingPurchase.quantity,
                        buyerName: name,
                        buyerDocument: document_,
                        buyerWhatsapp: whatsapp,
                        buyerAddress: address,
                        termsAccepted: true,
                        country: homePendingPurchase.country || null,
                        countryName: homePendingPurchase.countryName || null
                    })
                });

                const data = await response.json();
                
                if (data.success && data.url) {
                    showToast('Redirecionando para pagamento...', 'success');
                    setTimeout(() => window.location.href = data.url, 1000);
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro ao criar checkout', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro ao processar compra', 'error');
            }
        });

        // Recurrence Modal
        let selectedType = 'ipv6';
        let selectedPeriod = '1m';
        let periodMonths = 1;
        
        const PRICING = {
            ipv6:   { name: 'IPv6',         icon: 'ðŸŒ', price: 29.90, minQty: 1 },
            ipv4:   { name: 'IPv4',         icon: 'ðŸ–¥ï¸', price: 39.90, minQty: 1 },
            isp:    { name: 'ISP',          icon: 'ðŸ¢', price: 49.90, minQty: 1 },
            mobile: { name: 'Mobile 4G/5G', icon: 'ðŸ“±', price: 79.90, minQty: 1 }
        };

        const PERIODS = [
            { id: '1w', name: '1 Semana', months: 0.25, days: 7, discount: 0 },
            { id: '2w', name: '2 Semanas', months: 0.5, days: 14, discount: 0 },
            { id: '1m', name: '1 MÃªs', months: 1, days: 30, discount: 0 },
            { id: '2m', name: '2 Meses', months: 2, days: 60, discount: 0.10 },
            { id: '3m', name: '3 Meses', months: 3, days: 90, discount: 0.15 },
            { id: '6m', name: '6 Meses', months: 6, days: 180, discount: 0.25 },
            { id: '12m', name: '12 Meses', months: 12, days: 365, discount: 0.35 }
        ];

        function openRecurrenceModal(type, price, minQty) {
            selectedType = type;
            selectedPeriod = '1m';
            periodMonths = 1;
            
            const info = PRICING[type] || { name: type.toUpperCase(), icon: 'ðŸŒ', price, minQty };
            
            document.getElementById('recurrence-type-icon').textContent = info.icon;
            document.getElementById('recurrence-type-name').textContent = info.name;
            document.getElementById('recurrence-min-qty').textContent = `MÃ­nimo: ${info.minQty} proxy(s)`;
            document.getElementById('recurrence-quantity').min = info.minQty;
            document.getElementById('recurrence-quantity').value = info.minQty;
            
            renderPeriodOptions(info.price, info.minQty);
            updateRecurrenceTotal();
            
            openRecurrenceModalUI();
        }

        function renderPeriodOptions(price, minQty) {
            const container = document.getElementById('period-options');
            container.innerHTML = PERIODS.map(period => {
                const totalPrice = price * period.months * (1 - period.discount) * minQty;
                const hasDiscount = period.discount > 0;
                
                return `
                    <button onclick="selectPeriodOption('${period.id}', ${period.months}, ${price}, ${minQty})" 
                        class="period-btn p-3 rounded-xl text-left transition-all ${hasDiscount ? 'gradient-border' : ''}"
                        style="background: var(--bg-secondary); border: 1px solid var(--border-color)"
                        data-period="${period.id}">
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-1">
                            <span class="font-semibold text-sm" style="color: var(--text-primary)">${period.name}</span>
                            ${hasDiscount ? `<span class="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 text-green-400">-${(period.discount * 100).toFixed(0)}%</span>` : ''}
                        </div>
                        <span class="text-lg font-bold" style="color: var(--badge-text)">R$ ${totalPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}</span>
                    </button>
                `;
            }).join('');
            
            selectPeriodOption('1m', 1, price, minQty);
        }

        function selectPeriodOption(periodId, months, price, minQty) {
            selectedPeriod = periodId;
            periodMonths = months;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.period-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = 'var(--bg-secondary)';
            });
            
            const activeBtn = document.querySelector(`[data-period="${periodId}"]`);
            if (activeBtn) {
                activeBtn.style.borderColor = 'var(--badge-text)';
                activeBtn.style.background = 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1)';
            }
            
            updateRecurrenceTotal();
        }

        function updateRecurrenceTotal() {
            const price = PRICING[selectedType]?.price || 29.90;
            const quantity = parseInt(document.getElementById('recurrence-quantity').value) || PRICING[selectedType]?.minQty || 1;
            const period = PERIODS.find(p => p.id === selectedPeriod) || PERIODS[2];
            
            const subtotal = price * periodMonths * quantity;
            const discount = subtotal * period.discount;
            const total = subtotal - discount;
            
            document.getElementById('summary-period').textContent = period.name;
            document.getElementById('summary-total').textContent = `R$ ${total.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
        }

        function openRecurrenceModalUI() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('recurrence-modal');
            const content = modal.querySelector('.recurrence-modal-content');
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                content.classList.remove('scale-95', 'opacity-0');
                content.classList.add('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
            });
        }

        function closeRecurrenceModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('recurrence-modal');
            const content = modal.querySelector('.recurrence-modal-content');
            
            content.classList.add('scale-95', 'opacity-0');
            content.classList.remove('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                modal.classList.add('hidden');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
            }, 300);
        }

        function confirmRecurrence() {
            const quantity = parseInt(document.getElementById('recurrence-quantity').value) || PRICING[selectedType]?.minQty || 1;
            
            closeRecurrenceModal();
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                openCheckoutModalWithData(selectedType, selectedPeriod, quantity);
            }, 350);
        }

        function openCheckoutModalWithData(type, period, quantity) {
            const info = PRICING[type] || { name: type.toUpperCase(), price: 29.90 };
            const periodInfo = PERIODS.find(p => p.id === period) || PERIODS[2];
            const pricePerMonth = info.price * (1 - periodInfo.discount);
            
            currentType = type;
            currentPeriod = period;
            basePrice = pricePerMonth;
            
            const planNames = {
                '1w': '1 Semana',
                '2w': '2 Semanas',
                '1m': '1 MÃªs',
                '2m': '2 Meses',
                '3m': '3 Meses',
                '6m': '6 Meses',
                '12m': '12 Meses'
            };
            
            document.getElementById('modal-plan-name').textContent = `${info.name} - ${planNames[period]}`;
            document.getElementById('modal-quantity').textContent = `${quantity} proxy(s)`;
            document.getElementById('modal-total').textContent = `R$ ${(pricePerMonth * periodInfo.months * quantity).toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').value = quantity;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').min = info.minQty || 1;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').max = 100;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').disabled = true;
            
            document.getElementById('checkout-email').value = '';
            document.getElementById('checkout-whatsapp').value = '';
            
            openModal();
            updateTotal();
        }

        function getDiscount(quantity) {
            if (quantity >= 50) return 0.20;
            if (quantity >= 20) return 0.15;
            if (quantity >= 10) return 0.10;
            if (quantity >= 5) return 0.05;
            return 0;
        }

        function getDiscountText(quantity) {
            const discount = getDiscount(quantity);
            if (discount > 0) {
                return `ðŸŽ‰ ${Math.round(discount * 100)}% de desconto aplicado!`;
            }
            return `Adicione mais ${5 - quantity} proxies para ganhar 5% OFF`;
        }

        function openCheckoutModal(period, price) {
            currentPeriod = period;
            basePrice = price;
            
            const planNames = {
                'monthly': 'Plano Mensal',
                'annual': 'Plano Anual'
            };
            
            document.getElementById('modal-plan-name').textContent = planNames[period] || period;
            document.getElementById('modal-quantity').textContent = '1 proxy';
            document.getElementById('modal-total').textContent = `R$ ${price.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').value = 1;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').min = 1;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').max = 100;
            document.getElementById('proxy-count').disabled = false;
            
            document.getElementById('checkout-email').value = '';
            document.getElementById('checkout-whatsapp').value = '';
            
            openModal();
            updateTotal();
        }

        function openModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('checkout-modal');
            const content = modal.querySelector('.checkout-modal-content');
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                content.classList.remove('scale-95', 'opacity-0');
                content.classList.add('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
            });
        }

        function closeCheckoutModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('checkout-modal');
            const content = modal.querySelector('.checkout-modal-content');

            content.classList.add('scale-95', 'opacity-0');
            content.classList.remove('scale-100', 'opacity-100');

            setTimeout(() => {
                modal.classList.add('hidden');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
                // Reset coupon state on close
                removeCoupon();
            }, 300);
        }

        // Coupon state
        let appliedCouponCode = null;
        let appliedCouponDiscount = 0; // absolute R$ value

        function getRawTotal() {
            const quantity = parseInt(document.getElementById('proxy-count').value) || 1;
            const discount = getDiscount(quantity);
            const discountedPrice = basePrice * (1 - discount);
            return quantity * discountedPrice;
        }

        function updateTotal() {
            const quantity = parseInt(document.getElementById('proxy-count').value) || 1;
            const rawTotal = getRawTotal();
            const finalTotal = Math.max(0, rawTotal - appliedCouponDiscount);

            document.getElementById('modal-quantity').textContent = `${quantity} proxy${quantity > 1 ? 's' : ''}`;

            if (appliedCouponDiscount > 0) {
                document.getElementById('modal-total').innerHTML =
                    `<span style="text-decoration:line-through;opacity:.45;font-size:.9em;margin-right:6px">R$ ${rawTotal.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}</span>` +
                    `<span style="color:var(--badge-text)">R$ ${finalTotal.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}</span>`;
            } else {
                document.getElementById('modal-total').textContent = `R$ ${rawTotal.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            }

            const discountBadge = document.getElementById('discount-badge');
            const discountText = document.getElementById('discount-text');
            discountBadge.classList.remove('hidden');
            discountText.textContent = getDiscountText(quantity);
        }

        async function applyCoupon() {
            const code = (document.getElementById('checkout-coupon').value || '').trim().toUpperCase();
            const feedback = document.getElementById('coupon-feedback');
            const btn = document.getElementById('coupon-btn');

            if (!code) {
                showCouponFeedback('Informe o cÃ³digo do cupom', false);
                return;
            }

            // Reset if same code re-applied
            if (appliedCouponCode && appliedCouponCode === code) {
                showCouponFeedback(`Cupom "${code}" jÃ¡ estÃ¡ aplicado`, true);
                return;
            }

            btn.textContent = '...';
            btn.disabled = true;

            try {
                const orderValue = getRawTotal();
                const emailVal = (document.getElementById('checkout-email')?.value || '').trim();
                const res = await fetch('/api/coupons/validate-public', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ code, orderValue, email: emailVal || null })
                });
                const data = await res.json();

                if (data.success) {
                    appliedCouponCode = data.coupon.code;
                    appliedCouponDiscount = data.coupon.discount;

                    // Build feedback message â€” warn first_only customers
                    const isFirstOnly = data.coupon.scope === 'first_only';
                    const mainMsg = `âœ“ ${data.message}`;
                    showCouponFeedback(mainMsg, true, isFirstOnly);

                    // Style the input as applied
                    const input = document.getElementById('checkout-coupon');
                    input.style.borderColor = 'rgb(34,197,94)';
                    input.readOnly = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'âœ•';
                    btn.onclick = removeCoupon;
                    btn.style.borderColor = 'rgba(239,68,68,.5)';
                    btn.style.color = 'rgb(239,68,68)';
                } else {
                    appliedCouponCode = null;
                    appliedCouponDiscount = 0;
                    showCouponFeedback(data.message, false);
                    btn.textContent = 'Aplicar';
                    btn.disabled = false;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                showCouponFeedback('Erro ao validar cupom', false);
                btn.textContent = 'Aplicar';
                btn.disabled = false;
            }

            updateTotal();
        }

        function removeCoupon() {
            appliedCouponCode = null;
            appliedCouponDiscount = 0;
            const input = document.getElementById('checkout-coupon');
            input.value = '';
            input.readOnly = false;
            input.style.borderColor = '';
            const btn = document.getElementById('coupon-btn');
            btn.textContent = 'Aplicar';
            btn.disabled = false;
            btn.onclick = applyCoupon;
            btn.style.borderColor = '';
            btn.style.color = '';
            document.getElementById('coupon-feedback').classList.add('hidden');
            updateTotal();
        }

        function showCouponFeedback(msg, success, showFirstOnlyWarning = false) {
            const el = document.getElementById('coupon-feedback');
            el.classList.remove('hidden');
            el.style.background = success ? 'rgba(34,197,94,.1)' : 'rgba(239,68,68,.1)';
            el.style.color = success ? 'rgb(34,197,94)' : 'rgb(239,68,68)';
            el.style.border = `1px solid ${success ? 'rgba(34,197,94,.3)' : 'rgba(239,68,68,.3)'}`;
            if (showFirstOnlyWarning) {
                const fullPrice = basePrice ? `R$ ${basePrice.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}` : 'o valor cheio';
                el.innerHTML = `<div>${msg}</div>
                    <div style="margin-top:6px;padding:8px 10px;border-radius:8px;background:rgba(251,191,36,.12);border:1px solid rgba(251,191,36,.3);color:#fbbf24;font-size:0.78rem;line-height:1.45">
                        âš ï¸ <strong>Desconto vÃ¡lido apenas no 1Âº mÃªs.</strong><br>
                        A partir do 2Âº mÃªs vocÃª pagarÃ¡ o valor normal de <strong>${fullPrice}/proxy</strong>.
                    </div>`;
            } else {
                el.textContent = msg;
            }
        }

        async function handleCheckout(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('checkout-btn');
            const btnText = document.getElementById('checkout-btn-text');
            const spinner = document.getElementById('checkout-spinner');
            
            btn.disabled = true;
            btnText.textContent = 'Redirecionando...';
            spinner.classList.remove('hidden');
            
            const email = document.getElementById('checkout-email').value;
            const whatsapp = document.getElementById('checkout-whatsapp').value;
            const proxyCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('proxy-count').value);

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/stripe/create-checkout', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        email,
                        whatsapp,
                        proxyCount,
                        period: currentPeriod,
                        type: currentType,
                        couponCode: appliedCouponCode || null
                    })
                });
                
                const data = await response.json();
                
                if (data.success && data.checkoutUrl) {
                    // Store email for account creation after payment
                    localStorage.setItem('pendingAccountEmail', email);
                    localStorage.setItem('pendingAccountPeriod', currentPeriod);
                    localStorage.setItem('pendingAccountProxies', proxyCount);
                    localStorage.setItem('pendingAccountType', currentType);
                    window.location.href = data.checkoutUrl;
                } else {
                    alert(data.error || 'Erro ao processar checkout. Tente novamente.');
                    btn.disabled = false;
                    btnText.textContent = 'Continuar para Pagamento';
                    spinner.classList.add('hidden');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Checkout error:', error);
                alert('Erro de conexÃ£o. Verifique sua internet e tente novamente.');
                btn.disabled = false;
                btnText.textContent = 'Continuar para Pagamento';
                spinner.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }

        // Check URL params on load - for "buy more proxies" from portal
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            // Init pricing panel
            currentType          = 'ipv6';
            panelSelectedPeriod  = '1m';
            updatePurchasePanel();
            selectPanelPeriod('1m');
            
            const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            
            if (urlParams.get('checkout') === 'true') {
                const count = parseInt(urlParams.get('count')) || 1;
                const email = urlParams.get('email') || '';
                
                // Clear localStorage params
                localStorage.removeItem('buyMoreProxies');
                localStorage.removeItem('buyMoreCount');
                localStorage.removeItem('buyMoreEmail');
                
                // Open checkout with pre-filled data
                openCheckoutModal('monthly', 29.90);
                document.getElementById('proxy-count').value = count;
                document.getElementById('checkout-email').value = decodeURIComponent(email);
                updateTotal();
            }
        });

        // International Proxy Modal Functions
        let intlConfig = {
            country: null,
            countryName: '',
            type: null,
            typeName: '',
            typePrice: 0,
            period: '1m',
            periodDiscount: 0,
            quantity: 1
        };

        function openIntlModal() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('intl-modal');
            if (!modal) return;

                country: null,
                countryName: '',
                type: null,
                typeName: '',
                typePrice: 0,
                period: '1m',
                periodDiscount: 0,
                quantity: 1
            };
            
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            
            document.getElementById('intl-step-1').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('intl-step-2').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('intl-step-3').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('buy-home-intl-btn').disabled = true;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-country-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = '';
            });
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-type-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';

            });
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-period-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = 'var(--bg-secondary)';
            });
            
            document.getElementById('home-period-1m').style.borderColor = 'var(--badge-text)';
            document.getElementById('home-period-1m').style.background = 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1)';

            document.getElementById('intl-summary').textContent = '-';
            document.getElementById('home-intl-price').textContent = 'R$ 0,00';
            document.getElementById('home-intl-discount').textContent = '-R$ 0,00';
            document.getElementById('home-intl-total').textContent = 'R$ 0,00';
        }

        function closeIntlModal() {
            document.getElementById('intl-modal').classList.add('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function selectIntlCountry(code, name) {
            intlConfig.country = code;
            intlConfig.countryName = name;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-country-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = '';
            });
            
            event.currentTarget.style.borderColor = 'var(--badge-text)';
            event.currentTarget.style.background = 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1)';
            
            document.getElementById('intl-step-2').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('intl-step-3').classList.add('hidden');
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-type-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = '';
            });
            
            updateIntlSummary();
        }

        function selectIntlType(type) {
            intlConfig.type = type;
            intlConfig.typeName = INTL_TYPE_PRICES[type].name;
            intlConfig.typePrice = INTL_TYPE_PRICES[type].price;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-type-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = '';
            });
            
            event.currentTarget.style.borderColor = 'var(--badge-text)';
            event.currentTarget.style.background = 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1)';
            
            document.getElementById('intl-step-3').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('buy-home-intl-btn').disabled = false;
            
            document.getElementById('home-intl-qty').value = 1;
            intlConfig.quantity = 1;
            
            selectHomeIntlPeriod('1m', 0);
            updateHomeIntlPrice();
            updateIntlSummary();
        }

        function selectHomeIntlPeriod(periodId, discount) {
            intlConfig.period = periodId;
            intlConfig.periodDiscount = discount;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.intl-period-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                btn.style.background = 'var(--bg-secondary)';
            });
            
            const activeBtn = document.getElementById(`home-period-${periodId}`);
            if (activeBtn) {
                activeBtn.style.borderColor = 'var(--badge-text)';
                activeBtn.style.background = 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.1)';
            }
            
            updateHomeIntlPrice();
            updateIntlSummary();
        }

        function changeHomeIntlQty(delta) {
            const input = document.getElementById('home-intl-qty');
            const newVal = Math.max(1, parseInt(input.value || 1) + delta);
            input.value = newVal;
            intlConfig.quantity = newVal;
            updateHomeIntlPrice();
            updateIntlSummary();
        }

        function updateHomeIntlPrice() {
            const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('home-intl-qty').value) || 1;
            intlConfig.quantity = qty;
            
            const basePrice = intlConfig.typePrice || 0;
            const subtotal = basePrice * qty;
            const discount = subtotal * intlConfig.periodDiscount;
            const total = subtotal - discount;
            
            document.getElementById('home-intl-price').textContent = `R$ ${basePrice.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            document.getElementById('home-intl-discount').textContent = `-R$ ${discount.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
            document.getElementById('home-intl-total').textContent = `R$ ${total.toFixed(2).replace('.', ',')}`;
        }

        function updateIntlSummary() {
            const summary = `${intlConfig.countryName || '-'} - ${intlConfig.typeName || '-'}`;
            document.getElementById('intl-summary').textContent = summary;
        }

        function buyHomeIntlProxy() {
            if (!intlConfig.country || !intlConfig.type) {
                showToast('Complete todas as etapas', 'error');
                return;
            }

            homePendingPurchase = {
                type:        intlConfig.type,
                period:      intlConfig.period,
                quantity:    intlConfig.quantity,
                country:     intlConfig.country,
                countryName: intlConfig.countryName
            };

            closeIntlModal();
            openHomeTermsModal();
        }

        // ===== MOBILE PRICING BOTTOM-SHEET =====
        let msheetPeriod = '1m';

        function openMobilePricingSheet(type) {
            if (type === 'mobile') { showMobileComingSoon(); return; }
            currentType = type;
            // Update card highlights (same as desktop)
            document.querySelectorAll('.plan-type-card').forEach(card => {
                card.classList.remove('selected-type');
                card.style.borderColor = 'var(--border-color)';
                card.style.background  = 'var(--bg-card)';
            });
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`type-card-${type}`);
            if (activeCard) activeCard.classList.add('selected-type');

            const info = HOME_PRICING[type];

            // Header
            document.getElementById('msheet-icon').textContent = info.icon;
            document.getElementById('msheet-name').textContent = info.name;
            document.getElementById('msheet-price-tag').textContent = `R$${info.sellPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')} por proxy/mÃªs`;

            const badge = document.getElementById('msheet-delivery-badge');
            if (!info.autoDelivery) {
                badge.textContent = 'ðŸ“¦ Estoque';
                badge.className = 'text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold bg-green-500/20 text-green-400';
            } else {
                badge.textContent = 'âš¡ API Auto';
                badge.className = 'text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400';
            }

            // Qty
            const qtyEl = document.getElementById('msheet-qty');
            qtyEl.min = info.minQty;
            qtyEl.value = info.minQty;

            // Period reset
            msheetPeriod = '1m';
            selectMobilePeriod('1m');

            document.getElementById('mobile-pricing-sheet').classList.add('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }

        function closeMobilePricingSheet() {
            document.getElementById('mobile-pricing-sheet').classList.remove('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function selectMobilePeriod(id) {
            msheetPeriod = id;
            document.querySelectorAll('.msheet-period-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.period === id);
            });
            updateMobileTotal();
        }

        function changeMobileQty(delta) {
            const input  = document.getElementById('msheet-qty');
            const minVal = parseInt(input.min) || 1;
            input.value  = Math.max(minVal, parseInt(input.value || 1) + delta);
            updateMobileTotal();
        }

        function updateMobileTotal() {
            const info   = HOME_PRICING[currentType];
            const period = HOME_PERIODS.find(p => p.id === msheetPeriod) || HOME_PERIODS[0];
            const qty    = parseInt(document.getElementById('msheet-qty').value) || 1;

            const pricePerMonth = info.sellPrice * (1 - period.discount);
            const total         = pricePerMonth * period.months * qty;

            document.getElementById('msheet-total').textContent   = `R$ ${total.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}`;
            document.getElementById('msheet-per-proxy').textContent = `R$ ${info.sellPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}${period.discount > 0 ? ` (âˆ’${Math.round(period.discount*100)}%)` : ''}`;

            // Show/hide discount badge
            const discBadge = document.getElementById('msheet-discount-badge');
            if (period.discount > 0) {
                discBadge.textContent = `âˆ’${Math.round(period.discount*100)}% OFF`;
                discBadge.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                discBadge.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }

        function startMobilePurchase() {
            const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('msheet-qty').value) || 1;
            homePendingPurchase = {
                type:     currentType,
                period:   msheetPeriod,
                quantity: qty,
                months:   (HOME_PERIODS.find(p => p.id === msheetPeriod) || HOME_PERIODS[0]).months
            };
            // Keep sheet visible until terms modal opens
            closeMobilePricingSheet();
            openHomeTermsModal();
        }

        // Toast notification
        function showToast(message, type = 'info') {
            const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
            if (!toast) {
                console.log(message);
                return;
            }
            toast.textContent = message;
            toast.className = `fixed bottom-4 right-4 px-6 py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold z-50 ${type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white' : 'bg-green-500 text-black'}`;
            toast.classList.remove('hidden');
            setTimeout(() => toast.classList.add('hidden'), 3000);
        }
    </script>

        <p id="toast-msg" class="text-sm"></p>

    <!-- Modal -->
    <div id="modal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/90 hidden items-center justify-center z-50 p-4" onclick="closeModal()">
        <div class="bg-zinc-900 border border-white/20 rounded-2xl p-6 w-full max-w-md" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">
            <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
                <h3 class="text-xl font-bold text-white" id="modal-title"></h3>
                <button onclick="closeModal()" class="text-muted hover:text-white"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
