    <script>
        const API_URL = '';
        let token = localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_admin_token');

        // Theme toggle
        function toggleTheme() {
            const html = document.documentElement;
            const isDark = !html.classList.contains('light');
            const logo = document.getElementById('admin-logo');
            
            if (isDark) {
                html.classList.add('light');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
                if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/ymxkPNS0/LOGO-FAST-PROXY-black.png';
            } else {
                html.classList.remove('light');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
                if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/SwQ6ksRy/LOGO-FAST-PROXY.png';
            }
        }

        // Init theme on load
        function initTheme() {
            const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme');
            const html = document.documentElement;
            const logo = document.getElementById('admin-logo');
            
            if (savedTheme === 'light') {
                html.classList.add('light');
                if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/ymxkPNS0/LOGO-FAST-PROXY-black.png';
            } else if (savedTheme === 'dark') {
                html.classList.remove('light');
            } else if (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches) {
                html.classList.add('light');
                if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/ymxkPNS0/LOGO-FAST-PROXY-black.png';
            }
        }
        initTheme();

        function showTab(tab) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('bg-green-500/20', 'text-green-400');
                btn.classList.add('text-secondary');
            });
            
            const clickedBtn = document.querySelector(`.tab-btn[onclick="showTab('${tab}')"]`);
            if (clickedBtn) {
                clickedBtn.classList.remove('text-secondary');
                clickedBtn.classList.add('bg-green-500/20', 'text-green-400');
            }
            
            ['add', 'stock', 'users', 'coupons', 'logs', 'tutorials', 'blog'].forEach(t => {
                const el = document.getElementById(`tab-${t}`);
                if (el) el.classList.add('hidden');
            });
            const tabEl = document.getElementById(`tab-${tab}`);
            if (tabEl) tabEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            
            if (tab === 'stock') loadProxies();
            if (tab === 'users') loadUsers();
            if (tab === 'coupons') loadCoupons();
            if (tab === 'logs') { loadLogs(); loadLogStats(); }
            if (tab === 'tutorials') loadTutorials();
            if (tab === 'blog') loadPosts();
        }

        async function api(endpoint, method = 'GET', body = null) {
            const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
            if (token) headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;
            const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}${endpoint}`, { method, headers, body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : null });
            return res.json();
        }

        function showToast(msg, type = 'success') {
            const div = document.getElementById('toast');
            document.getElementById('toast-msg').textContent = msg;
            div.className = `fixed bottom-6 right-6 card rounded-xl p-4 border-${type === 'success' ? 'green' : 'red'}-500/50`;
            div.classList.remove('hidden');
            setTimeout(() => div.classList.add('hidden'), 3000);
        }

        async function handleLogin(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const btn = document.getElementById('login-btn');
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner spin mr-2"></i>Entrando...';
            
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/login', 'POST', {
                    email: document.getElementById('login-email').value,
                    password: document.getElementById('login-password').value
                });
                if (data.success && data.user.role === 'admin') {
                    token = data.token;
                    localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_admin_token', token);
                    document.getElementById('login-section').classList.add('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('dashboard').classList.remove('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('admin-name').textContent = data.user.name;
                    loadStats();
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('login-error').textContent = data.message || 'Credenciais invÃ¡lidas';
                    document.getElementById('login-error').classList.remove('hidden');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                document.getElementById('login-error').textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o';
                document.getElementById('login-error').classList.remove('hidden');
            }
            btn.innerHTML = 'Entrar';
        }

        // Coupons Functions
        function selectScope(val) {
            const allLabel   = document.getElementById('scope-all-label');
            const firstLabel = document.getElementById('scope-first-label');
            const active   = 'border-green-500/60 bg-green-500/10';
            const inactive = 'border-white/10 bg-white/5';
            if (val === 'all') {
                document.getElementById('scope-all').checked = true;
                allLabel.className   = allLabel.className.replace(inactive, active);
                firstLabel.className = firstLabel.className.replace(active, inactive);
            } else {
                document.getElementById('scope-first').checked = true;
                firstLabel.className = firstLabel.className.replace(inactive, active);
                allLabel.className   = allLabel.className.replace(active, inactive);
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('coupon-form')?.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const code    = document.getElementById('coupon-code').value.trim();
            const percent = document.getElementById('coupon-percent').value;
            const amount  = document.getElementById('coupon-amount').value;
            const days    = document.getElementById('coupon-days').value;
            const max     = document.getElementById('coupon-max').value;
            const scope   = document.querySelector('input[name="coupon-scope"]:checked')?.value || 'all';

            try {
                const result = await api('/api/subscription/admin/coupons/create', 'POST', {
                    code,
                    discount_percent: percent || null,
                    discount_amount: amount || null,
                    valid_days: days || null,
                    max_uses: max || null,
                    scope
                });

                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('Cupom criado!', 'success');
                    this.reset();
                    selectScope('all'); // reset scope UI
                    loadCoupons();
                } else {
                    showToast(result.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro', 'error');
            }
        });

        async function loadCoupons() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/coupons');
                const coupons = data.coupons || [];
                const list = document.getElementById('coupons-list');
                
                if (coupons.length > 0) {
                    list.innerHTML = coupons.map(c => {
                        const scopeTag = c.scope === 'first_only'
                            ? `<span style="background:rgba(251,191,36,.15);color:#fbbf24;border:1px solid rgba(251,191,36,.3)" class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs">1Âª compra</span>`
                            : `<span style="background:rgba(34,197,94,.1);color:#4ade80;border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,.2)" class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs">Todas</span>`;
                        const expiry = c.valid_until ? ` | Expira: ${new Date(c.valid_until).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}` : '';
                        return `<div class="flex justify-between items-center p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-lg gap-2">
                            <div class="min-w-0">
                                <div class="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                                    <span class="font-bold font-mono">${c.code}</span>
                                    ${scopeTag}
                                    ${c.is_active ? '' : '<span class="text-xs text-red-400">Inativo</span>'}
                                </div>
                                <div class="text-xs text-secondary mt-1">
                                    ${c.discount_percent ? c.discount_percent + '% off' : 'R$ ' + parseFloat(c.discount_amount).toFixed(2) + ' off'}
                                    &nbsp;Â·&nbsp; Usado: ${c.used_count}${c.max_uses ? '/'+c.max_uses : ''}${expiry}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <button onclick="deleteCoupon(${c.id})" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 flex-shrink-0"><i class="fas fa-trash"></i></button>
                        </div>`;
                    }).join('');
                } else {
                    list.innerHTML = '<p class="text-secondary text-center py-4">Nenhum cupom</p>';
                }
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        async function deleteCoupon(id) {
            if (!confirm('Excluir cupom?')) return;
            const result = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/coupons/${id}`, 'DELETE');
            if (result.success) { showToast('Cupom deletado'); loadCoupons(); }
        }

        // Access Logs Functions
        async function loadLogs() {
            try {
                const userId = document.getElementById('log-user-id').value;
                const startDate = document.getElementById('log-start-date').value;
                const endDate = document.getElementById('log-end-date').value;
                
                let endpoint = '/api/accesslogs/admin/logs?limit=100';
                if (userId) endpoint += `&userId=${userId}`;
                if (startDate && endDate) endpoint += `&startDate=${startDate}&endDate=${endDate}`;
                
                const data = await api(endpoint);
                const logs = data.logs || [];
                const tbody = document.getElementById('logs-table');
                
                if (logs.length > 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = logs.map(l => `<tr class="border-t border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <div class="font-medium">${l.email || 'N/A'}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs opacity-50">${l.name || ''}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${l.proxy_ip || 'N/A'}:${l.proxy_port || ''}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-mono">${l.client_ip || 'N/A'}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${l.target_host || 'N/A'}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${l.request_method || 'N/A'}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${l.connected_at ? new Date(l.connected_at).toLocaleString('pt-BR') : 'N/A'}</td>
                    </tr>`).join('');
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-secondary">Nenhum registro encontrado</td></tr>';
                }
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        async function loadLogStats() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/accesslogs/admin/stats');
                const stats = data.stats;
                if (stats) {
                    document.getElementById('stat-total-connections').textContent = stats.total_conexoes || 0;
                    document.getElementById('stat-active-users').textContent = stats.usuarios_ativos || 0;
                    document.getElementById('stat-proxies-used').textContent = stats.proxies_utilizados || 0;
                    document.getElementById('stat-unique-ips').textContent = stats.ips_unicos_acesso || 0;
                }
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        async function searchLogs() {
            await loadLogs();
            await loadLogStats();
        }

        function exportLogs() {
            const userId = document.getElementById('log-user-id').value;
            const startDate = document.getElementById('log-start-date').value;
            const endDate = document.getElementById('log-end-date').value;
            
            let url = '/api/accesslogs/admin/export';
            const params = [];
            if (userId) params.push(`userId=${userId}`);
            if (startDate) params.push(`startDate=${startDate}`);
            if (endDate) params.push(`endDate=${endDate}`);
            if (params.length > 0) url += '?' + params.join('&');
            
            window.open(url, '_blank');
        }

        function logout() {
            token = null;
            localStorage.removeItem('fastproxy_admin_token');
            document.getElementById('login-section').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('dashboard').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        async function loadStats() {
            try {
                const [pData, uData] = await Promise.all([
                    api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies'),
                    api('/api/subscription/admin/users')
                ]);
                const proxies = pData.data?.proxies || [];
                const users = uData.data?.users || [];
                const activeProxies = proxies.filter(p => p.is_active).length;
                const availableProxies = proxies.filter(p => !p.user_id).length;
                
                document.getElementById('stat-total').textContent = proxies.length;
                document.getElementById('stat-available').textContent = availableProxies;
                document.getElementById('stat-active').textContent = activeProxies;
                document.getElementById('stat-users').textContent = users.length;
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        function parseProxy(proxyStr) {
            const match = proxyStr.match(/^([^:]+):([^@]+)@(.+):(\d+)$/);
            if (!match) return null;
            return { username: match[1], password: match[2], ip: match[3], port: parseInt(match[4]) };
        }

        async function addSingleProxy(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const proxyStr = document.getElementById('single-proxy').value.trim();
            const tier = document.getElementById('single-tier').value;
            const proxy = parseProxy(proxyStr);
            
            if (!proxy) {
                showToast('Formato invÃ¡lido. Use: user:pass@ip:port', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies', 'POST', { ...proxy, tier });
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Proxy adicionado!');
                    document.getElementById('single-proxy').value = '';
                    loadStats();
                    loadProxies();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error'); }
        }

        async function addBulkProxy(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const lines = document.getElementById('bulk-proxies').value.trim().split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
            const tier = document.getElementById('bulk-tier').value;
            const proxies = lines.map(l => parseProxy(l.trim())).filter(p => p);
            
            if (proxies.length === 0) {
                showToast('Nenhum proxy vÃ¡lido encontrado', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies/bulk', 'POST', { proxies, tier });
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast(`${data.data?.count || proxies.length} proxies importados!`);
                    document.getElementById('bulk-proxies').value = '';
                    document.getElementById('bulk-count').textContent = '0';
                    loadStats();
                    loadProxies();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error'); }
        }

        async function loadProxies() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies');
                const proxies = data.data?.proxies || [];
                const tbody = document.getElementById('proxies-table');
                
                if (proxies.length > 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = proxies.map(p => `<tr class="border-t border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 w-10"><input type="checkbox" class="proxy-checkbox w-4 h-4 accent-green-500" value="${p.id}"></td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-sm">${p.username}:${p.password}@${p.ip}:${p.port}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm ${p.is_active ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'}">${p.is_active ? 'Ativo' : 'Inativo'}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">
                            ${p.user_email ? `<div class="text-white">${p.user_email}</div>` : '<span class="text-white/30">NÃ£o vinculado</span>'}
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-secondary">
                            ${new Date(p.created_at).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">
                            ${!p.user_id ? `<button onclick="allocateThisProxy('${p.id}', '${p.username}:${p.password}@${p.ip}:${p.port}')" class="text-green-400 hover:text-green-300 mr-2" title="Vincular"><i class="fas fa-link"></i></button>` : ''}
                            <button onclick="deleteProxy('${p.id}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300" title="Excluir"><i class="fas fa-trash"></i></button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join('');
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-muted">Nenhum proxy</td></tr>';
                }
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        function toggleSelectAll() {
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.proxy-checkbox');
            const selectAll = document.getElementById('select-all-proxies').checked || document.getElementById('select-all-top').checked;
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = selectAll);
        }

        async function executeBulkAction() {
            const action = document.getElementById('bulk-action').value;
            const selected = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.proxy-checkbox:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
            
            if (selected.length === 0) {
                showToast('Selecione pelo menos um proxy', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            if (action === 'delete') {
                if (!confirm(`Excluir ${selected.length} proxy(s)?`)) return;
                for (const id of selected) {
                    await api(`/api/subscription/admin/proxies/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                }
                showToast(`${selected.length} proxy(s) excluÃ­do(s)`);
            } else if (action === 'available') {
                // Return to stock (remove user/subscription association)
                for (const id of selected) {
                    await api(`/api/subscription/admin/proxies/${id}`, 'PUT', { returnToStock: true });
                }
                showToast(`${selected.length} proxy(s) devolvido(s) ao estoque`);
            }
            
            loadProxies();
            loadStats();
        }

        async function deleteProxy(id) {
            if (!confirm('Excluir proxy?')) return;
            try {
                const data = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/proxies/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Proxy excluÃ­do');
                    loadStats();
                    loadProxies();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error'); }
        }

        async function allocateThisProxy(proxyId, proxyStr) {
            try {
                const usersData = await api('/api/subscription/admin/users');
                const users = usersData.data?.users || [];
                
                if (users.length === 0) {
                    showToast('Nenhum usuÃ¡rio cadastrado', 'error');
                    return;
                }
                
                const userList = users.map(u => `<div class="user-option flex items-center justify-between p-3 hover:bg-white/5 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition" onclick="selectUser('${u.id}', '${u.name || ''}', '${u.email}', '${u.whatsapp || ''}')">
                    <div>
                        <div class="font-medium text-white">${u.name || 'Sem nome'}</div>
                        <div class="text-sm text-secondary">${u.email}</div>
                        ${u.whatsapp ? `<div class="text-xs text-green-400">${u.whatsapp}</div>` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-xs text-white/30">${u.proxy_count || 0} proxies</div>
                </div>`).join('');
                
                document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = 'Vincular Proxy';
                document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = `
                    <div class="space-y-4">
                        <div class="p-3 bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30 rounded-lg font-mono text-sm text-green-400">${proxyStr}</div>
                        <div>
                            <input type="text" id="user-search" placeholder="Buscar por email..." class="input-field w-full rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-white" oninput="searchUsersByEmail(this.value)">
                        </div>
                        <div id="user-list" class="max-h-60 overflow-y-auto space-y-1">
                            ${userList}
                        </div>
                        <div id="selected-user" class="hidden p-3 bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30 rounded-lg">
                            <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
                                <div>
                                    <div class="font-medium text-white" id="sel-user-name"></div>
                                    <div class="text-sm text-secondary" id="sel-user-email"></div>
                                </div>
                                <button onclick="clearUser()" class="text-secondary hover:text-white"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-sm text-secondary mb-2">Email do usuÃ¡rio</label>
                            <input type="email" id="allocate-user-email" placeholder="usuario@email.com" class="input-field w-full rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-white">
                        </div>
                        <button onclick="confirmAllocateByEmail('${proxyId}')" class="btn-primary w-full py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold text-white">
                            <i class="fas fa-link mr-2"></i>Vincular por Email
                        </button>
                    </div>
                `;
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro', 'error'); }
        }

        function filterUsers() {
            const search = document.getElementById('user-search').value.toLowerCase();
            const options = document.querySelectorAll('.user-option');
            options.forEach(opt => {
                const text = opt.innerText.toLowerCase();
                opt.classList.toggle('hidden', !text.includes(search));
            });
        }
        
        async function searchUsersByEmail(email) {
            if (email.length < 3) return;
            try {
                const data = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/users/by-email/${encodeURIComponent(email)}`);
                const users = data.data?.users || [];
                const userList = document.getElementById('user-list');
                if (users.length > 0) {
                    userList.innerHTML = users.map(u => `<div class="user-option flex items-center justify-between p-3 hover:bg-white/5 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition" onclick="selectUser('${u.id}', '${u.name || ''}', '${u.email}', '${u.whatsapp || ''}')">
                        <div>
                            <div class="font-medium text-white">${u.name || 'Sem nome'}</div>
                            <div class="text-sm text-secondary">${u.email}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-xs text-white/30">${u.proxy_count || 0} proxies</div>
                    </div>`).join('');
                } else {
                    userList.innerHTML = '<div class="p-3 text-center text-secondary">Nenhum usuÃ¡rio encontrado</div>';
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
            }
        }

        function selectUser(id, name, email, whatsapp) {
            document.getElementById('allocate-user-id').value = id;
            document.getElementById('sel-user-name').textContent = name;
            document.getElementById('sel-user-email').textContent = email;
            document.getElementById('user-list').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('selected-user').classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        function clearUser() {
            document.getElementById('allocate-user-id').value = '';
            document.getElementById('user-list').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('selected-user').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        async function confirmAllocate(proxyId) {
            const userId = document.getElementById('allocate-user-id').value;
            
            if (!userId) {
                showToast('Selecione um usuÃ¡rio', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies/allocate', 'POST', {
                    proxyId,
                    userId
                });
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Proxy vinculado!');
                    closeModal();
                    loadProxies();
                    loadStats();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error'); }
        }
        
        async function confirmAllocateByEmail(proxyId) {
            const email = document.getElementById('allocate-user-email').value.trim();
            
            if (!email) {
                showToast('Digite o email do usuÃ¡rio', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/proxies/allocate', 'POST', {
                    proxyId,
                    email
                });
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Proxy vinculado a ' + email + '!');
                    closeModal();
                    loadProxies();
                    loadStats();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error'); }
        }

        function closeModal() {
            document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        async function loadUsers() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/users');
                const users = data.data?.users || [];
                const tbody = document.getElementById('users-table');
                
                if (users.length > 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = users.map(u => `<tr class="border-t border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <div class="font-medium">${u.name || 'N/A'}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs opacity-50">${u.email}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${u.whatsapp || '-'}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm">${u.proxy_count || 0}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs bg-green-500/20 text-green-400">Ativo</span></td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm opacity-50">${new Date(u.created_at).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">
                            <button onclick="allocateProxy('${u.id}', '${u.email}')" class="text-blue-400 hover:text-blue-300 mr-2"><i class="fas fa-plus"></i></button>
                            <button onclick="cancelSubscription('${u.id}', '${u.email}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300" title="Cancelar assinatura"><i class="fas fa-ban"></i></button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join('');
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-muted">Nenhum usuÃ¡rio</td></tr>';
                }
            } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
        }

        async function viewUserProxies(userId) {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/users');
                const users = data.data?.users || [];
                const user = users.find(u => u.id == userId);
                if (!user) {
                    showToast('UsuÃ¡rio nÃ£o encontrado', 'error');
                    return;
                }
                showToast(`UsuÃ¡rio: ${user.email}\nProxies: ${user.proxy_count || 0}`);
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro ao carregar', 'error');
            }
        }

        async function cancelSubscription(userId, userEmail) {
            const confirmed = confirm(`Tem certeza que deseja cancelar a assinatura de ${userEmail}?\n\nClique OK para oferecer cupom de 50% de desconto ou Cancelar para cancelar sem desconto.`);
            
            if (!confirmed) {
                try {
                    await api(`/api/subscription/admin/users/${userId}/cancel`, 'POST', { applyCoupon: false });
                    showToast('Assinatura cancelada');
                    loadUsers();
                } catch (err) {
                    showToast('Erro ao cancelar', 'error');
                }
                return;
            }
            
            const modalContent = `
                <div class="space-y-4">
                    <div class="p-4 rounded-xl bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30">
                        <p class="text-white font-medium mb-2">Deseja aplicar um cupom de <span class="text-green-400 font-bold">50% de desconto</span>?</p>
                        <p class="text-sm text-secondary">Isso reduz o valor da prÃ³xima renovaÃ§Ã£o pela metade.</p>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="flex gap-3">
                        <button onclick="applyCancellationCoupon('${userId}', true)" class="flex-1 py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-500 text-white transition">
                            <i class="fas fa-ticket-alt mr-2"></i>Sim, aplicar 50%
                        </button>
                        <button onclick="applyCancellationCoupon('${userId}', false)" class="flex-1 py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-500 text-white transition">
                            <i class="fas fa-times mr-2"></i>Cancelar direto
                        </button>
                    </div>
                    
                    <button onclick="closeModal()" class="w-full py-2 text-secondary hover:text-white transition text-sm">
                        Voltar
                    </button>
                </div>
            `;
            
            document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('items-center');
            document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = 'Cancelar Assinatura';
            document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = modalContent;
        }

        async function applyCancellationCoupon(userId, applyCoupon) {
            try {
                const data = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/users/${userId}/cancel`, 'POST', { 
                    applyCoupon,
                    discountPercent: applyCoupon ? 50 : 0
                });
                
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast(applyCoupon ? 'Cupom 50% aplicado!' : 'Assinatura cancelada');
                    closeModal();
                    loadUsers();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error');
            }
        }

        function allocateProxy(userId, userEmail) {
            // Open modal for allocation - fill email field
            const modalContent = `
                <div class="space-y-4">
                    <div class="p-4 bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/30 rounded-lg">
                        <p class="text-white font-medium">Vincular proxy ao usuÃ¡rio:</p>
                        <p class="text-green-400">${userEmail}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <label class="block text-sm text-secondary mb-2">Email do usuÃ¡rio</label>
                        <input type="email" id="allocate-user-email-modal" value="${userEmail}" class="input-field w-full rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-white">
                    </div>
                    <button onclick="confirmAllocateToUser()" class="btn-primary w-full py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold">
                        <i class="fas fa-link mr-2"></i>Vincular Proxy
                    </button>
                </div>
            `;
            
            document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = 'Vincular Proxy';
            document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = modalContent;
            
            showToast('Selecione um proxy disponÃ­vel na lista e clique em Vincular');
            loadProxies();
        }
        
        async function confirmAllocateToUser() {
            const email = document.getElementById('allocate-user-email-modal')?.value;
            if (!email) {
                showToast('Email nÃ£o encontrado', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            // Show proxies list to select
            showToast('Clique no botÃ£o Vincular ao lado do proxy que deseja alocar a ' + email);
        }

        document.getElementById('bulk-proxies').addEventListener('input', function() {
            const count = this.value.trim().split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).length;
            document.getElementById('bulk-count').textContent = count;
        });

        // Tutorials functions
        function generateSlug(title, existingSlug) {
            const slug = title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
            document.getElementById('tutorial-slug').value = slug;
        }

        document.getElementById('tutorial-title')?.addEventListener('input', function() {
            generateSlug(this.value);
        });

        document.getElementById('tutorial-form')?.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const data = {
                title: document.getElementById('tutorial-title').value,
                slug: document.getElementById('tutorial-slug').value,
                category: document.getElementById('tutorial-category').value,
                icon: document.getElementById('tutorial-icon').value,
                status: document.getElementById('tutorial-status').value,
                excerpt: document.getElementById('tutorial-excerpt').value,
                content: document.getElementById('tutorial-content').value,
                image_url: document.getElementById('tutorial-image').value
            };
            
            try {
                const result = await api('/api/subscription/admin/tutorials', 'POST', data);
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('Tutorial salvo!');
                    this.reset();
                    loadTutorials();
                } else {
                    showToast(result.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error');
            }
        });

        async function loadTutorials() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/tutorials');
                const tutorials = data.tutorials || [];
                const tbody = document.getElementById('tutorials-table');
                
                if (tutorials.length > 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = tutorials.map(t => `<tr class="border-t border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <div class="font-medium">${t.title}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs opacity-50">/${t.slug}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm capitalize">${t.category}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <span class="px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs ${t.status === 'published' ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'}">
                                ${t.status === 'published' ? 'Publicado' : 'Rascunho'}
                            </span>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm opacity-50">${new Date(t.created_at).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">
                            <button onclick="editTutorial(${t.id})" class="text-blue-400 hover:text-blue-300 mr-2"><i class="fas fa-edit"></i></button>
                            <button onclick="deleteTutorial(${t.id})" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300"><i class="fas fa-trash"></i></button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join('');
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-muted">Nenhum tutorial</td></tr>';
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
            }
        }

        async function editTutorial(id) {
            const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/tutorials');
            const tutorial = data.tutorials?.find(t => t.id === id);
            if (!tutorial) return;
            
            document.getElementById('tutorial-title').value = tutorial.title;
            document.getElementById('tutorial-slug').value = tutorial.slug;
            document.getElementById('tutorial-category').value = tutorial.category || 'configuracao';
            document.getElementById('tutorial-icon').value = tutorial.icon || 'book';
            document.getElementById('tutorial-status').value = tutorial.status || 'draft';
            document.getElementById('tutorial-excerpt').value = tutorial.excerpt || '';
            document.getElementById('tutorial-content').value = tutorial.content || '';
            document.getElementById('tutorial-image').value = tutorial.image_url || '';
            
            showToast('Editando tutorial - faÃ§a suas alteraÃ§Ãµes e salve');
            
            const form = document.getElementById('tutorial-form');
            form.onsubmit = async function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const result = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/tutorials/${id}`, 'PUT', {
                    title: document.getElementById('tutorial-title').value,
                    slug: document.getElementById('tutorial-slug').value,
                    category: document.getElementById('tutorial-category').value,
                    icon: document.getElementById('tutorial-icon').value,
                    status: document.getElementById('tutorial-status').value,
                    excerpt: document.getElementById('tutorial-excerpt').value,
                    content: document.getElementById('tutorial-content').value,
                    image_url: document.getElementById('tutorial-image').value
                });
                
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('Tutorial atualizado!');
                    form.reset();
                    form.onsubmit = null;
                    document.getElementById('tutorial-form').addEventListener('submit', arguments.callee);
                    loadTutorials();
                } else {
                    showToast(result.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            };
        }

        async function deleteTutorial(id) {
            if (!confirm('Excluir tutorial?')) return;
            try {
                const data = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/tutorials/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Tutorial excluÃ­do');
                    loadTutorials();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error');
            }
        }

        // Blog posts functions
        function generatePostSlug(title) {
            const slug = title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
            document.getElementById('post-slug').value = slug;
        }

        document.getElementById('post-title')?.addEventListener('input', function() {
            generatePostSlug(this.value);
        });

        document.getElementById('post-form')?.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const data = {
                title: document.getElementById('post-title').value,
                slug: document.getElementById('post-slug').value,
                category: document.getElementById('post-category').value,
                status: document.getElementById('post-status').value,
                excerpt: document.getElementById('post-excerpt').value,
                content: document.getElementById('post-content').value,
                image_url: document.getElementById('post-image').value,
                meta_title: document.getElementById('post-meta-title').value,
                meta_description: document.getElementById('post-meta-desc').value
            };
            
            try {
                const result = await api('/api/subscription/admin/posts', 'POST', data);
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('Post salvo!');
                    this.reset();
                    loadPosts();
                } else {
                    showToast(result.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error');
            }
        });

        async function loadPosts() {
            try {
                const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/posts');
                const posts = data.posts || [];
                const tbody = document.getElementById('posts-table');
                
                if (posts.length > 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = posts.map(p => `<tr class="border-t border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <div class="font-medium">${p.title}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs opacity-50">/${p.slug}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm capitalize">${p.category}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3">
                            <span class="px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs ${p.status === 'published' ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'}">
                                ${p.status === 'published' ? 'Publicado' : 'Rascunho'}
                            </span>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-sm opacity-50">${new Date(p.created_at).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}</td>
                        <td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">
                            <button onclick="editPost(${p.id})" class="text-blue-400 hover:text-blue-300 mr-2"><i class="fas fa-edit"></i></button>
                            <button onclick="deletePost(${p.id})" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300"><i class="fas fa-trash"></i></button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`).join('');
                } else {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-muted">Nenhum post</td></tr>';
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
            }
        }

        async function editPost(id) {
            const data = await api('/api/subscription/admin/posts');
            const post = data.posts?.find(p => p.id === id);
            if (!post) return;
            
            document.getElementById('post-title').value = post.title;
            document.getElementById('post-slug').value = post.slug;
            document.getElementById('post-category').value = post.category || 'geral';
            document.getElementById('post-status').value = post.status || 'draft';
            document.getElementById('post-excerpt').value = post.excerpt || '';
            document.getElementById('post-content').value = post.content || '';
            document.getElementById('post-image').value = post.image_url || '';
            document.getElementById('post-meta-title').value = post.meta_title || '';
            document.getElementById('post-meta-desc').value = post.meta_description || '';
            
            showToast('Editando post - faÃ§a suas alteraÃ§Ãµes e salve');
            
            const form = document.getElementById('post-form');
            form.onsubmit = async function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const result = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/posts/${id}`, 'PUT', {
                    title: document.getElementById('post-title').value,
                    slug: document.getElementById('post-slug').value,
                    category: document.getElementById('post-category').value,
                    status: document.getElementById('post-status').value,
                    excerpt: document.getElementById('post-excerpt').value,
                    content: document.getElementById('post-content').value,
                    image_url: document.getElementById('post-image').value,
                    meta_title: document.getElementById('post-meta-title').value,
                    meta_description: document.getElementById('post-meta-desc').value
                });
                
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('Post atualizado!');
                    form.reset();
                    form.onsubmit = null;
                    document.getElementById('post-form').addEventListener('submit', arguments.callee);
                    loadPosts();
                } else {
                    showToast(result.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            };
        }

        async function deletePost(id) {
            if (!confirm('Excluir post?')) return;
            try {
                const data = await api(`/api/subscription/admin/posts/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                if (data.success) {
                    showToast('Post excluÃ­do');
                    loadPosts();
                } else {
                    showToast(data.message || 'Erro', 'error');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o', 'error');
            }
        }

        // Load admin check on page load
        if (token) {
            api('/api/subscription/me').then(data => {
                if (data.success && data.user) {
                    document.getElementById('login-section').classList.add('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('dashboard').classList.remove('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('admin-name').textContent = data.user.name || data.user.email;
                    loadStats();
                }
            }).catch(() => {
                localStorage.removeItem('fastproxy_admin_token');
                token = null;
            });
        }
    </script>
</body>

<script>
// â”€â”€ Constants â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

const PM_PRICING = {
    ipv6: { name:'IPv6',  icon:'ðŸŒ', sellPrice:29.90, minQty:1 },

};
const PM_PERIODS = [
    { id:'1m',  months:1,  discount:0    },
