const PERIOD_NAMES = { '1m':'1 MÃªs','6m':'6 Meses','12m':'12 Meses','1w':'1 Sem','2w':'2 Sem','3m':'3 Meses',monthly:'Mensal',annual:'Anual' };

// â”€â”€ State â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
let token           = localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_token');
let currentUser     = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_user')         || 'null');
let currentSubscription = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_subscription') || 'null');
let currentProxies  = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_proxies')      || '[]');
let selectedProxyId = null;
let pendingResetToken = null;
let pollIntervalRef = null;  // for polling pending proxies

// Plans modal state
let pmType   = 'ipv6';
let pmPeriod = '1m';

// â”€â”€ Init â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    initTheme();

    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

    // Check for password reset token in URL
    const resetToken = urlParams.get('reset_token');
    if (resetToken) {
        pendingResetToken = resetToken;
        showTab('reset');
        return; // Don't auto-login, show reset form
    }

    if (token && currentUser) {
        showDashboard();
        loadUserData().then(() => {
            // Auto-poll for ProxySeller API delivery every 60s regardless of pending status
            startAutoPoll();
        });

        const welcomeType = urlParams.get('welcome');
        if (welcomeType) {
            const banner  = document.getElementById('welcome-banner');
            const titleEl = document.getElementById('welcome-title');
            const subEl   = document.getElementById('welcome-subtitle');
            if (welcomeType === 'new') {
                titleEl.textContent = 'Conta criada e pagamento confirmado! ðŸŽ‰';
                subEl.textContent   = 'Bem-vindo ao FastProxy! Seus proxies estÃ£o prontos abaixo.';
            } else {
                titleEl.textContent = 'Pagamento confirmado! âœ…';
                subEl.textContent   = 'Seus proxies foram ativados. Confira abaixo.';
            }
            banner.classList.remove('hidden');
            setTimeout(() => banner.classList.add('hidden'), 8000);
            window.history.replaceState({}, '', '/portal.html');
        }
    }
});

// â”€â”€ Theme â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function toggleTheme() {
    const html = document.documentElement;
    const logo = document.getElementById('portal-logo');
    if (!html.classList.contains('light')) {
        html.classList.add('light');
        localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
        if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/ymxkPNS0/LOGO-FAST-PROXY-black.png';
    } else {
        html.classList.remove('light');
        localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
        if (logo) logo.src = 'https://i.ibb.co/SwQ6ksRy/LOGO-FAST-PROXY.png';
    }
}
function initTheme() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('theme');
    const html  = document.documentElement;
    if (saved === 'light') html.classList.add('light');
    else if (!saved && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches) html.classList.add('light');
}

// â”€â”€ Tabs â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function showTab(tab) {
    ['login','register','forgot','reset'].forEach(t => {
        const btn  = document.getElementById(`tab-${t}`);
        const form = document.getElementById(`${t}-form`);
        const isActive = t === tab;
        if (btn)  btn.className  = isActive
            ? 'flex-1 pb-3 text-center font-medium text-green-400 border-b-2 border-green-400 text-sm'
            : 'flex-1 pb-3 text-center font-medium text-secondary border-b-2 border-transparent hover:text-white transition text-sm';
        if (form) form.classList.toggle('hidden', !isActive);
    });
    // Show reset tab button if needed
    const resetTab = document.getElementById('tab-reset');
    if (tab === 'reset' && !resetTab) {
        // Just show the form
    }
}

// â”€â”€ Auth â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
async function handleLogin(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email    = document.getElementById('login-email').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('login-password').value;
    const errDiv   = document.getElementById('login-error');
    const btn      = document.getElementById('login-btn');

    errDiv.classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('login-btn-txt').textContent = 'Entrandoâ€¦';
    document.getElementById('login-spin').classList.remove('hidden');
    btn.disabled = true;

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/login`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (data.success) {
            token = data.token;
            currentUser = data.user;
            currentProxies = data.proxies || [];

            let subs = [];
            if (data.subscription) {
                subs = [{
                    id: data.subscription.id, period: data.subscription.period,
                    proxyCount: data.subscription.proxyCount, status: data.subscription.status,
                    startDate: data.subscription.startDate, endDate: data.subscription.endDate,
                    isActive: data.hasActiveSubscription
                }];
            }
            currentSubscription = { hasActiveSubscription: data.hasActiveSubscription || currentProxies.length > 0, subscriptions: subs };

            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_token',        token);
            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_user',         JSON.stringify(currentUser));
            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_subscription', JSON.stringify(currentSubscription));
            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_proxies',      JSON.stringify(currentProxies));

            showDashboard();
            renderDashboard();
        } else {
            errDiv.textContent = data.message || 'Credenciais invÃ¡lidas';
            errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
            resetLoginBtn();
        }
    } catch {
        errDiv.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o. Verifique sua internet.';
        errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
        resetLoginBtn();
    }
}
function resetLoginBtn() {
    document.getElementById('login-btn-txt').textContent = 'Entrar';
    document.getElementById('login-spin').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('login-btn').disabled = false;
}

async function handleRegister(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email    = document.getElementById('reg-email').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('reg-password').value;
    const confirm  = document.getElementById('reg-password-confirm').value;
    const whatsapp = document.getElementById('reg-whatsapp').value;
    const errDiv   = document.getElementById('register-error');

    if (password !== confirm) { errDiv.textContent = 'As senhas nÃ£o coincidem.'; errDiv.classList.remove('hidden'); return; }
    if (password.length < 6)  { errDiv.textContent = 'Senha deve ter â‰¥ 6 caracteres.'; errDiv.classList.remove('hidden'); return; }

    errDiv.classList.add('hidden');

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/register`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({ email, password, whatsapp })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (data.success) {
            token = data.token; currentUser = data.user;
            currentProxies = []; currentSubscription = null;
            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_token', token);
            localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser));
            showToast('Conta criada! Assine um plano para receber seus proxies.', 'success');
            showDashboard();
            renderDashboard();
        } else {
            errDiv.textContent = data.message || 'Erro ao criar conta';
            errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    } catch {
        errDiv.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o.';
        errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
    }
}

async function handleForgotPassword(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const email  = document.getElementById('forgot-email').value.trim();
    const msgEl  = document.getElementById('forgot-message');
    const btn    = document.getElementById('forgot-btn');
    msgEl.classList.add('hidden');

    document.getElementById('forgot-btn-txt').textContent = 'Enviandoâ€¦';
    document.getElementById('forgot-spin').classList.remove('hidden');
    btn.disabled = true;

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/forgot-password`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({ email })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        msgEl.textContent = data.message || 'Email enviado!';
        msgEl.className = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-green-500/15 border border-green-500/25 text-green-400';
        msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
    } catch {
        msgEl.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o. Tente novamente.';
        msgEl.className = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-red-500/15 border border-red-500/25 text-red-400';
        msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
    } finally {
        document.getElementById('forgot-btn-txt').textContent = 'Enviar link de recuperaÃ§Ã£o';
        document.getElementById('forgot-spin').classList.add('hidden');
        btn.disabled = false;
    }
}

async function handleResetPassword(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const newPwd  = document.getElementById('reset-password').value;
    const confirm = document.getElementById('reset-password-confirm').value;
    const msgEl   = document.getElementById('reset-message');

    if (newPwd !== confirm) {
        msgEl.textContent = 'As senhas nÃ£o coincidem.';
        msgEl.className   = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-red-500/15 border border-red-500/25 text-red-400';
        msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        return;
    }

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/reset-password`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({ token: pendingResetToken, newPassword: newPwd })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (data.success) {
            msgEl.textContent = data.message;
            msgEl.className   = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-green-500/15 border border-green-500/25 text-green-400';
            msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            pendingResetToken = null;
            window.history.replaceState({}, '', '/portal.html');
            setTimeout(() => showTab('login'), 2500);
        } else {
            msgEl.textContent = data.message || 'Erro ao redefinir senha.';
            msgEl.className   = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-red-500/15 border border-red-500/25 text-red-400';
            msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    } catch {
        msgEl.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o.';
        msgEl.className   = 'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-red-500/15 border border-red-500/25 text-red-400';
        msgEl.classList.remove('hidden');
    }
}

function showDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('login-section').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard-section').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('nav-user').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('nav-user').classList.add('flex');
    document.getElementById('nav-email').textContent = currentUser?.email || '';
}

function logout() {
    token = null; currentUser = null; currentSubscription = null; currentProxies = [];
    ['fastproxy_token','fastproxy_user','fastproxy_subscription','fastproxy_proxies'].forEach(k => localStorage.removeItem(k));
    document.getElementById('login-section').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard-section').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('nav-user').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('nav-user').classList.remove('flex');
}

function togglePassword(id) {
    const inp = document.getElementById(id);
    inp.type = inp.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
}

// â”€â”€ renderDashboard â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function renderDashboard() {
    // 1. Name
    const nameEl = document.getElementById('user-name');
    if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = currentUser?.name || currentUser?.email?.split('@')[0] || 'usuÃ¡rio';

    // 2. Resolve subscription
    let sub = null, hasActive = false;
    if (currentSubscription) {
        if (currentSubscription.subscriptions && Array.isArray(currentSubscription.subscriptions)) {
            sub = currentSubscription.subscriptions.find(s => s.isActive || s.status === 'active')
               || currentSubscription.subscriptions[0] || null;
            hasActive = !!currentSubscription.hasActiveSubscription;
        } else if (currentSubscription.subscription?.id) {
            sub = currentSubscription.subscription;
            hasActive = !!currentSubscription.hasActiveSubscription || sub.status === 'active';
        } else if (currentSubscription.id && currentSubscription.period) {
            sub = currentSubscription;
            hasActive = sub.status === 'active';
        }
    }

    const qty      = sub?.proxyCount || sub?.proxy_count || currentProxies.length || 0;
    const period   = PERIOD_NAMES[sub?.period] || sub?.period || 'â€”';
    const endRaw   = sub?.endDate   || sub?.end_date;
    const startRaw = sub?.startDate || sub?.start_date;
    const endFmt   = endRaw   ? new Date(endRaw).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')   : 'â€”';
    const startFmt = startRaw ? new Date(startRaw).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR') : 'â€”';

    // 3. Subtitle
    const subInfoEl = document.getElementById('subscription-info');
    if (subInfoEl) {
        if (sub && hasActive) subInfoEl.textContent = `${qty} proxy${qty !== 1?'s':''} â€¢ Plano ${period} â€¢ vence ${endFmt}`;
        else if (currentProxies.length > 0) subInfoEl.textContent = `${currentProxies.length} proxy${currentProxies.length !== 1?'s':''} ativo${currentProxies.length!==1?'s':''}`;
        else subInfoEl.textContent = 'Sem assinatura ativa.';
    }

    // 4. Subscription details card
    const subDetailsEl = document.getElementById('subscription-details');
    if (subDetailsEl) {
        if (sub) {
            const statusHtml = (sub.status === 'active' || hasActive)
                ? '<span class="font-semibold text-green-400">âœ“ Ativo</span>'
                : `<span class="text-red-400 capitalize">${sub.status || 'â€”'}</span>`;
            subDetailsEl.innerHTML = `
                <div class="flex justify-between py-1.5"><span class="text-secondary">Plano</span><span class="font-medium">${period}</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between py-1.5"><span class="text-secondary">Proxies</span><span class="font-medium">${qty}</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between py-1.5"><span class="text-secondary">InÃ­cio</span><span class="font-medium">${startFmt}</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between py-1.5"><span class="text-secondary">Vencimento</span><span class="font-medium">${endFmt}</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between py-1.5"><span class="text-secondary">Status</span>${statusHtml}</div>
                <div class="mt-3 pt-3" style="border-top:1px solid var(--border-color)">
                    <a href="/cancelar.html" class="text-xs flex items-center gap-1 transition" style="color:rgba(239,68,68,0.7)" onmouseover="this.style.color='#f87171'" onmouseout="this.style.color='rgba(239,68,68,0.7)'">
                        <i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Cancelar assinatura
                    </a>
                </div>
            `;
        } else {
            subDetailsEl.innerHTML = `<p class="text-secondary text-sm">Nenhuma assinatura ativa.</p>`;
        }
    }

    // 5. Update action card text
    const actionTitle = document.getElementById('action-title');
    const actionDesc  = document.getElementById('action-desc');
    const openLabel   = document.getElementById('open-plans-label');
    if (!sub && currentProxies.length === 0) {
        if (actionTitle) actionTitle.textContent = 'Assinar um Plano';
        if (actionDesc)  actionDesc.textContent  = 'Escolha um tipo de proxy e comece agora.';
        if (openLabel)   openLabel.textContent   = 'Ver Planos e PreÃ§os';
    } else {
        if (actionTitle) actionTitle.textContent = 'Adicionar Proxies';
        if (actionDesc)  actionDesc.textContent  = 'Compre mais proxies para o seu account.';
        if (openLabel)   openLabel.textContent   = 'Comprar Mais Proxies';
    }

    // 6. Expiration check
    const expAlert = document.getElementById('expiration-alert');
    if (expAlert && sub && endRaw) {
        const daysLeft = Math.ceil((new Date(endRaw) - new Date()) / (1000*60*60*24));
        if (daysLeft <= 5 && daysLeft > 0) expAlert.classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    // 7. Render proxies
    renderProxies(hasActive || currentProxies.length > 0);
}

// â”€â”€ loadUserData â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
async function loadUserData() {
    const t = localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_token');
    if (!t) { logout(); return; }

    // Show cached data fast
    const storedUser  = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_user')         || 'null');
    const storedSub   = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_subscription') || 'null');
    const storedProxy = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fastproxy_proxies')      || '[]');
    if (storedUser || storedSub || storedProxy.length > 0) {
        currentUser = storedUser || currentUser;
        currentProxies = storedProxy.length > 0 ? storedProxy : currentProxies;
        currentSubscription = storedSub || currentSubscription;
        renderDashboard();
    }

    // Then refresh from server
    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/me`, { headers:{ Authorization:`Bearer ${t}` } });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (!data.success) { if (res.status === 401) logout(); return; }

        currentUser         = data.user;
        currentProxies      = data.proxies || [];
        currentSubscription = data;

        localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_user',         JSON.stringify(currentUser));
        localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_proxies',      JSON.stringify(currentProxies));
        localStorage.setItem('fastproxy_subscription', JSON.stringify(data));

        renderDashboard();

        if (data.discounts?.length > 0) {
            const d = data.discounts[0];
            document.getElementById('discount-details').textContent = `Desconto de ${d.discountPercent}% disponÃ­vel para renovaÃ§Ã£o!`;
            document.getElementById('discount-banner').classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error('loadUserData error:', err);
    }
}

// â”€â”€ renderProxies â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function renderProxies(hasActive = true) {
    const list = document.getElementById('proxies-list');

    if (!currentProxies || currentProxies.length === 0) {
        list.innerHTML = `
            <div class="text-center py-10">
                <div class="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl mx-auto mb-4 flex items-center justify-center" style="background:rgba(34,197,94,0.08); border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,0.15)">
                    <i class="fas fa-lock text-green-400 text-2xl"></i>
                </div>
                <p class="font-semibold mb-1">${hasActive ? 'Nenhum proxy encontrado' : 'Assinatura necessÃ¡ria'}</p>
                <p class="text-secondary text-sm mb-4">${hasActive ? 'Seus proxies aparecerÃ£o aqui apÃ³s a compra.' : 'Assine um plano para receber seus proxies agora.'}</p>
                <button onclick="openPlansModal()" class="btn-primary px-5 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-sm font-semibold inline-flex items-center gap-2">
                    <i class="fas fa-shopping-cart"></i>
                    ${hasActive ? 'Comprar Proxies' : 'Assinar Agora'}
                </button>
            </div>
        `;
        return;
    }

    // Build "copy all" block + individual proxy cards
    const allLine = currentProxies.map(p => `${p.username}:${p.password}@${p.ip}:${p.port}`).join('\n');

    list.innerHTML = `
        <div class="rounded-xl p-3.5 mb-2 flex items-center justify-between" style="background:rgba(34,197,94,0.07); border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,0.2)">
            <span class="text-sm font-semibold text-green-400"><i class="fas fa-layer-group mr-2"></i>Copiar todos (${currentProxies.length} proxies)</span>
            <button onclick="copyAllProxies()" class="text-xs font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition" style="background:#22c55e; color:#000;">
                <i class="fas fa-copy mr-1"></i> Copiar
            </button>
        </div>
    ` + currentProxies.map((p, idx) => {
        const proxyLine = p.line || `${p.username}:${p.password}@${p.ip}:${p.port}`;
        const createdDate = p.createdAt ? new Date(p.createdAt).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR') : '';
        const isPending = p.ip?.includes('pending') || p.username === 'pending';
        return `
        <div class="proxy-card p-4">
            <div class="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <div class="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1.5 flex-wrap">
                        <span class="w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0" style="background:${isPending?'#fbbf24':'#22c55e'}"></span>
                        <span class="text-xs font-mono" style="color:var(--text-secondary)">${p.ip}:${p.port}</span>
                        ${createdDate ? `<span class="text-xs" style="color:var(--text-muted)">${createdDate}</span>` : ''}
                        ${isPending ? '<span class="text-xs font-semibold text-yellow-400 bg-yellow-400/10 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">â³ Provisionando</span>' : ''}
                    </div>
                    <code class="text-xs text-green-400 break-all select-all">${proxyLine}</code>
                </div>
                <div class="flex gap-1.5 flex-shrink-0">
                    <button onclick='copyProxyLine(${JSON.stringify(proxyLine)})'
                        class="p-2 rounded-lg transition hover:bg-green-500/10"
                        style="background:var(--bg-secondary); border:1px solid var(--border-color)"
                        title="Copiar">
                        <i class="fas fa-copy text-xs text-green-400"></i>
                    </button>
                    ${!isPending ? `
                    <button onclick="openReplaceModal(${p.id})"
                        id="swap-btn-${p.id}"
                        class="px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-semibold transition flex items-center gap-1.5"
                        style="background:var(--bg-secondary); border:1px solid var(--border-color); color:var(--text-secondary)"
                        title="Trocar IP">
                        <i class="fas fa-sync-alt text-xs"></i>
                        <span>Trocar IP</span>
                        <span id="swap-price-${p.id}" class="swap-price-badge hidden">...</span>
                    </button>` : ''}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    }).join('');

    // â”€â”€ Provisioning poll: if any pending proxies, call poll endpoint every 30s
    if (pollIntervalRef) { clearInterval(pollIntervalRef); pollIntervalRef = null; }
    const hasPending = currentProxies.some(p => p.ip?.includes('pending') || p.username === 'pending');
    if (hasPending && token) {
        pollIntervalRef = setInterval(() => fetchProxiesFromAPI(), 30000);
        // First poll immediately
        setTimeout(() => fetchProxiesFromAPI(), 3000);
    }

    // Eagerly load swap prices for subscribed users
    const subId = currentSubscription?.subscriptions?.[0]?.id
               || currentSubscription?.subscription?.id
               || currentSubscription?.id;
    if (subId) {
        fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/replacement-price/${subId}`, {
            headers:{ Authorization:`Bearer ${token}` }
        }).then(r=>r.json()).then(data => {
            if (data.price) {
                currentProxies.forEach(p => {
                    const badge = document.getElementById(`swap-price-${p.id}`);
                    if (badge) {
                        badge.textContent = `R$${data.price.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}`;
                        badge.classList.remove('hidden');
                    }
                    // Also store for the modal
                    p._swapPrice      = data.price;
                    p._swapDays       = data.daysSinceStart;
                });
            }
        }).catch(()=>{});
    }
}

function copyAllProxies() {
    const text = currentProxies.map(p => `${p.username}:${p.password}@${p.ip}:${p.port}`).join('\n');
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => showToast(`${currentProxies.length} proxies copiados!`, 'success')).catch(() => showToast('Erro ao copiar','error'));
}

function copyProxyLine(line) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(line).then(() => showToast('Proxy copiado!','success')).catch(() => showToast('Erro ao copiar','error'));
}

function refreshProxies() {
    loadUserData();
    showToast('Atualizando dadosâ€¦', 'info');
}

// Auto-poll for ProxySeller proxy delivery (every 60s)
function startAutoPoll() {
    if (!token) return;
    // First poll after 30s, then every 60s
    setTimeout(() => {
        fetchProxiesFromAPI();
        // Continue polling every 60s
        pollIntervalRef = setInterval(fetchProxiesFromAPI, 60000);
    }, 30000);
}

async function fetchProxiesFromAPI() {
    if (!token) return;
    fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/fetch-proxies`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` }
    }).then(r => r.json()).then(data => {
        if (data.success && data.fetched > 0) {
            showToast(`âœ¨ ${data.fetched} proxy(s) prontos!`, 'success');
            // Stop polling since we got new proxies
            if (pollIntervalRef) { clearInterval(pollIntervalRef); pollIntervalRef = null; }
            // Reload user data to get updated proxy list
            loadUserData();
        } else if (data.success && data.provisioning) {
            // Still provisioning, update timer
            updateProvisioningTimer(data.message || 'Proxies sendo provisionados...');
        }
    }).catch(() => {});
}

function updateProvisioningTimer(message) {
    const existing = document.getElementById('provisioning-toast');
    if (existing) existing.querySelector('p').textContent = message;
}

// â”€â”€ Replace proxy modal â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function openReplaceModal(proxyId) {
    selectedProxyId = proxyId;
    const proxy = currentProxies.find(p => p.id === proxyId);

    // Update price display
    const priceDisplay  = document.getElementById('replace-price-display');
    const priceReason   = document.getElementById('replace-price-reason');
    const replacePoints = document.getElementById('replace-points');

    if (proxy?._swapPrice) {
        priceDisplay.textContent = `R$ ${proxy._swapPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}`;
        const days = proxy._swapDays || 0;
        priceReason.textContent = days <= 3 ? `${days} dias de uso (1â€“3 dias: R$1,99)`
                                : days <= 7 ? `${days} dias de uso (4â€“7 dias: R$5,99)`
                                :             `${days} dias de uso (8+ dias: R$11,99)`;
    } else {
        priceDisplay.textContent = 'R$ 1,99 â€“ R$ 11,99';
        priceReason.textContent = 'PreÃ§o varia conforme dias de uso';

        // Try fetching if we don't have cached price
        const subId = currentSubscription?.subscriptions?.[0]?.id || currentSubscription?.id;
        if (subId) {
            fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/replacement-price/${subId}`, {
                headers:{ Authorization:`Bearer ${token}` }
            }).then(r=>r.json()).then(data => {
                if (data.price) {
                    priceDisplay.textContent = `R$ ${data.price.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}`;
                    const d = data.daysSinceStart || 0;
                    priceReason.textContent = `${d} dias de uso`;
                }
            }).catch(()=>{});
        }
    }

    // Check reward points
    fetch(`${API_URL}/api/rewards/balance`, { headers:{ Authorization:`Bearer ${token}` } })
        .then(r=>r.json())
        .then(data => {
            if (data.success && data.points?.available >= 100) {
                document.getElementById('replace-points-avail').textContent = data.points.available;
                replacePoints.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                replacePoints.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }).catch(()=> replacePoints.classList.add('hidden'));

    document.getElementById('replace-error').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('replace-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
}

function closeReplaceModal() {
    document.getElementById('replace-modal').classList.add('hidden');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
    selectedProxyId = null;
}

async function swapWithPoints() {
    if (!selectedProxyId) return;
    const reason = document.getElementById('replace-reason').value;
    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/replace-proxy`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json', Authorization:`Bearer ${token}`},
            body: JSON.stringify({ proxyId:selectedProxyId, reason, usePoints:true })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.success) {
            showToast('Proxy trocado grÃ¡tis com pontos! ðŸŽ‰','success');
            closeReplaceModal(); loadUserData();
        } else { showToast(data.message || 'Erro ao trocar','error'); }
    } catch { showToast('Erro de conexÃ£o','error'); }
}

async function openCheckoutSwap() {
    if (!selectedProxyId) return;
    const reason = document.getElementById('replace-reason').value;
    const errDiv = document.getElementById('replace-error');
    errDiv.classList.add('hidden');

    const btn = document.getElementById('swap-pay-btn');
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-circle-notch spinner mr-2"></i>Redirecionandoâ€¦';

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/stripe/create-swap-checkout`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json', Authorization:`Bearer ${token}`},
            body: JSON.stringify({ proxyId:selectedProxyId, reason, email:currentUser?.email })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (data.success && data.url) {
            window.location.href = data.url;
        } else {
            errDiv.textContent = data.message || 'Erro ao criar checkout';
            errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
            btn.disabled = false;
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-credit-card mr-2"></i>Pagar e Trocar IP';
        }
    } catch {
        errDiv.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o.';
        errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-credit-card mr-2"></i>Pagar e Trocar IP';
    }
}

// â”€â”€ Plans modal â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function openPlansModal() {
    pmType   = 'ipv6';
    pmPeriod = '1m';
    document.querySelectorAll('.plan-type-card-portal').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
    document.getElementById('pm-card-ipv6').classList.add('selected');
    document.querySelectorAll('.period-btn-portal').forEach(b => {
        b.classList.toggle('selected', b.dataset.period === '1m');
    });
    document.getElementById('pm-qty').value = 1;
    document.getElementById('pm-error').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('pm-delivery-warn').classList.add('hidden');

    const pmBuyBtn  = document.getElementById('pm-buy-btn');
    const pmBuyTxt  = document.getElementById('pm-buy-txt');
    const pmBuySpin = document.getElementById('pm-buy-spin');
    pmBuyBtn.disabled = false;
    pmBuyTxt.textContent = 'Comprar Agora';
    pmBuySpin.classList.add('hidden');

    updatePMTotal();
    document.getElementById('plans-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
}

function closePlansModal() {
    document.getElementById('plans-modal').classList.add('hidden');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
}

function selectPMType(type) {
    pmType = type;
    document.querySelectorAll('.plan-type-card-portal').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
    document.getElementById(`pm-card-${type}`)?.classList.add('selected');
    const warn = document.getElementById('pm-delivery-warn');
    if (type === 'ipv6') {
        warn?.classList.add('hidden');
    } else {
        warn?.classList.remove('hidden');
    }
    updatePMTotal();
}

function selectPMPeriod(id) {
    pmPeriod = id;
    document.querySelectorAll('.period-btn-portal').forEach(b => {
        b.classList.toggle('selected', b.dataset.period === id);
    });
    updatePMTotal();
}

function changePMQty(delta) {
    const input  = document.getElementById('pm-qty');
    const minVal = PM_PRICING[pmType]?.minQty || 1;
    input.value  = Math.max(minVal, parseInt(input.value || 1) + delta);
    updatePMTotal();
}

function updatePMTotal() {
    const info   = PM_PRICING[pmType];
    const period = PM_PERIODS.find(p => p.id === pmPeriod) || PM_PERIODS[0];
    const qty    = parseInt(document.getElementById('pm-qty').value) || 1;

    const pricePerMonth = info.sellPrice * (1 - period.discount);
    const total         = pricePerMonth * period.months * qty;

    document.getElementById('pm-total').textContent    = `R$ ${total.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}`;
    document.getElementById('pm-per-proxy').textContent = `R$ ${info.sellPrice.toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}${period.discount>0?` (âˆ’${Math.round(period.discount*100)}%)`:''}`;
}

async function startPMPurchase() {
    const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('pm-qty').value) || 1;
    const errDiv  = document.getElementById('pm-error');
    const btn     = document.getElementById('pm-buy-btn');
    const btnTxt  = document.getElementById('pm-buy-txt');
    const btnSpin = document.getElementById('pm-buy-spin');

    errDiv.classList.add('hidden');
    btn.disabled = true;
    btnTxt.textContent = 'Criando checkoutâ€¦';
    btnSpin.classList.remove('hidden');

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/stripe/create-checkout`, {
            method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({
                email:      currentUser?.email,
                type:       pmType,
                period:     pmPeriod,
                proxyCount: qty
            })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (data.success && data.checkoutUrl) {
            window.location.href = data.checkoutUrl;
        } else {
            errDiv.textContent = data.error || data.message || 'Erro ao criar checkout.';
            errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
            btn.disabled = false;
            btnTxt.textContent = 'Comprar Agora';
            btnSpin.classList.add('hidden');
        }
    } catch {
        errDiv.textContent = 'Erro de conexÃ£o. Tente novamente.';
        errDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
        btn.disabled = false;
        btnTxt.textContent = 'Comprar Agora';
        btnSpin.classList.add('hidden');
    }
}

// â”€â”€ History â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
let historyLoaded = false;

function toggleHistory() {
    const panel  = document.getElementById('history-panel');
    const isOpen = !panel.classList.contains('hidden');
    panel.classList.toggle('hidden', isOpen);

    if (!isOpen && !historyLoaded) loadHistory();
}

async function loadHistory() {
    const panel   = document.getElementById('history-panel');
    const loading = document.getElementById('history-loading');
    const content = document.getElementById('history-content');

    loading.classList.remove('hidden');
    content.innerHTML = '';

    try {
        const res  = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/subscription/history`, {
            headers:{ Authorization:`Bearer ${token}` }
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        loading.classList.add('hidden');

        if (!data.success || !data.history?.length) {
            content.innerHTML = '<p class="text-secondary text-sm py-2">Nenhuma transaÃ§Ã£o encontrada.</p>';
            return;
        }

        const STATUS_CLASS = { active:'status-active', cancelled:'status-cancelled', expired:'status-expired' };
        const STATUS_LABEL = { active:'Ativo', cancelled:'Cancelado', expired:'Expirado', paid:'Pago' };

        content.innerHTML = data.history.map(h => `
            <div class="history-item">
                <div class="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p class="text-sm font-medium truncate">${h.description}</p>
                    <p class="text-xs mt-0.5" style="color:var(--text-muted)">
                        ${new Date(h.date).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}
                        ${h.endDate ? ` Â· atÃ© ${new Date(h.endDate).toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')}` : ''}
                    </p>
                </div>
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
                    <span class="text-sm font-bold text-green-400">R$ ${(h.amount||0).toFixed(2).replace('.',',')}</span>
                    <span class="status-badge ${STATUS_CLASS[h.status] || 'status-expired'}">${STATUS_LABEL[h.status] || h.status}</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        `).join('');

        historyLoaded = true;
    } catch {
        loading.classList.add('hidden');
        content.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-400 text-sm py-2">Erro ao carregar histÃ³rico.</p>';
    }
}

// â”€â”€ Misc â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
function useRenewalDiscount() {
    openPlansModal();
}

function redeemPoints() {
    showToast('Em breve: resgate de pontos por proxies grÃ¡tis!','info');
}

function showToast(message, type = 'info') {
    const container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
    const toast = document.createElement('div');
    const colors = { success:'border-green-500 text-green-400', error:'border-red-500 text-red-400', info:'border-blue-500 text-blue-400' };
    toast.className = `toast card p-3.5 flex items-center gap-2 ${colors[type] || colors.info}`;
    toast.style.minWidth = '220px';
    toast.innerHTML = `
        <i class="fas ${type==='success'?'fa-check-circle':type==='error'?'fa-times-circle':'fa-info-circle'} flex-shrink-0"></i>
        <p class="text-sm">${message}</p>
    `;
    container.appendChild(toast);
    setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity='0'; toast.style.transition='opacity 0.3s'; setTimeout(()=>toast.remove(),300); }, 3500);
}

// Close modals on backdrop click
document.getElementById('replace-modal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeReplaceModal();
});
document.getElementById('plans-modal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closePlansModal();
});
</script>
